08/10/2023, 17:48 - Sankhayan: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

typedef struct Node {
    int data;
    struct Node* next;
    struct Node* prev;
} Node;

// Function to create a new node
Node* createNode(int data) {
    Node* newNode = (Node*)malloc(sizeof(Node));
    if (newNode == NULL) {
        printf("Memory allocation failed.\n");
        exit(1);
    }
    newNode->data = data;
    newNode->next = NULL;
    newNode->prev = NULL;
    return newNode;
}

// Function to insert a node at the middle of the doubly linked list
void insertInMiddle(Node* head, int data) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        printf("The linked list is empty.\n");
        return;
    }

    Node* slow = head;
    Node* fast = head;

    while (fast != NULL && fast->next != NULL) {
        fast = fast->next->next;
        slow = slow->next;
    }

    Node* newNode = createNode(data);
    newNode->next = slow->next;
    newNode->prev = slow;
    if (slow->next != NULL)
        slow->next->prev = newNode;
    slow->next = newNode;
}

// Function to delete a node at a given position
void deleteNode(Node* head, int position) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        printf("The linked list is empty.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (position < 0) {
        printf("Invalid position.\n");
        return;
    }

    Node* current = head;
    int count = 0;

    while (current != NULL && count < position) {
        current = current->next;
        count++;
    }

    if (current == NULL) {
        printf("Invalid position.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (current->prev != NULL)
        current->prev->next = current->next;

    if (current->next != NULL)
        current->next->prev = current->prev;

    free(current);
}

// Function to traverse and print the doubly linked list
void traverse(Node* head) {
    Node* current = head;
    printf("Doubly Linked list: ");
    while (current != NULL) {
        printf("%d -> ", current->data);
        current = current->next;
    }
    printf("NULL\n");
}

int main() {
    Node* head = createNode(1);
    Node* second = createNode(2);
    Node* third = createNode(3);

    head->next = second;
    second->prev = head;
    second->next = third;
    third->prev = second;

    traverse(head);

    insertInMiddle(head, 4);
    traverse(head);

    deleteNode(head, 1);
    traverse(head);

    // Free allocated memory
    free(head);
    free(second);
    free(third);

    return 0;
}
08/10/2023, 17:48 - Sankhayan: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

typedef struct Node {
    int data;
    struct Node* next;
} Node;

// Function to create a new node
Node* createNode(int data) {
    Node* newNode = (Node*)malloc(sizeof(Node));
    if (newNode == NULL) {
        printf("Memory allocation failed.\n");
        exit(1);
    }
    newNode->data = data;
    newNode->next = NULL;
    return newNode;
}

// Function to insert a node at the middle of the circular linked list
void insertInMiddle(Node* head, int data) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        printf("The linked list is empty.\n");
        return;
    }

    Node* slow = head;
    Node* fast = head;

    // Move fast pointer by 2 and slow pointer by 1
    while (fast->next != head && fast->next->next != head) {
        fast = fast->next->next;
        slow = slow->next;
    }

    Node* newNode = createNode(data);
    newNode->next = slow->next;
    slow->next = newNode;
}

// Function to delete a node at a given position
void deleteNode(Node** head, int position) {
    if (*head == NULL) {
        printf("The linked list is empty.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (position < 0) {
        printf("Invalid position.\n");
        return;
    }

    Node* current = *head;
    Node* previous = NULL;
    int count = 0;

    // Find the node at the specified position
    do {
        previous = current;
        current = current->next;
        count++;
    } while (current != *head && count < position);

    if (current == *head && count != position) {
        printf("Invalid position.\n");
        return;
    }

    if (previous == NULL) {
        // If the head is being deleted
        Node* lastNode = *head;
        while (lastNode->next != *head)
            lastNode = lastNode->next;

        *head = current->next;
        lastNode->next = *head;
    } else {
        previous->next = current->next;
    }

    free(current);
}

// Function to traverse and print the circular linked list
void traverse(Node* head) {
    if (head == NULL) {
        printf("The linked list is empty.\n");
        return;
    }

    Node* current = head;
    printf("Circular Linked list: ");
    do {
        printf("%d -> ", current->data);
        current = current->next;
    } while (current != head);
    printf("\n");
}

int main() {
    Node* head = createNode(1);
    Node* second = createNode(2);
    Node* third = createNode(3);

    head->next = second;
    second->next = third;
    third->next = head;

    traverse(head);

    insertInMiddle(head, 4);
    traverse(head);

    deleteNode(&head, 1);
    traverse(head);

    // Free allocated memory
    free(head);
    free(second);
    free(third);

    return 0;
}

Without electricity, I couldn't watch TV or play video games, so I decided to spend time outside. I played games like hide-and-seek, and football with my friends. We also built a fort using old blankets and pillows. In the evening, we used flashlights to tell ghost stories. Since we couldn't use the oven my mother used a stove for dinner. It was interesting to see the stars clearly without any streetlights. I missed tv but I had a great time. I enjoyed spending time with my friends. <This message was edited>
